<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:0in;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:0in;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Item 1.01&#160; </font></b><b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Entry into a Material
Definitive Agreement.</font></b></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The information set forth in Item 2.03 is hereby incorporated by
reference into this Item 1.01.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:0in;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Item 2.03&#160; Creation of
a Direct Financial Obligation or an Obligation Under an Off-Balance Sheet
Arrangement of a Registrant.</font></b></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">On December 21, 2004, we entered into a lease agreement with
CarrAmerica Realty, L.P., pursuant to which we will lease up to approximately
82,000 square feet of real estate space in San Diego, California consisting of
laboratory and office space.&#160; The lease
commences on the latter of September 1, 2005, or the date that certain
landlord-funded tenant improvements are satisfactorily completed, and has an
initial term of 10 years unless extended or sooner terminated pursuant to the
terms of the lease.&#160; We have options to
extend the lease beyond 10 years consisting of two renewal periods of five
years each on terms contained in the lease.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Our aggregate lease payments as contemplated by the lease through 2015,
if there is no delay in the rent commencement date, will be approximately
$28,000,000.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in 12.0pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The foregoing summary of the lease agreement is qualified in its
entirety by reference to the lease agreement which is attached hereto as
Exhibit 99.1 and is hereby incorporated by reference into this Item 2.03.</font></p>

<p style="margin-left:0in;margin-right:0in;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Item 9.01&nbsp; Financial
Statements and Exhibits.</font></b></p>

<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:auto;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">LEASE</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:auto;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">THIS
LEASE (the &#147;<u>Lease</u>&#148;) is made as of December&nbsp;21, 2004, between <b><font style="font-weight:bold;">CARRAMERICA REALTY, L.P.</font></b>, a Delaware
limited partnership, (&#147;<u>Landlord</u>&#148;) and the tenant as named as &#147;<u>Tenant</u>&#148;
in the Schedule&nbsp;below.&#160; The term &#147;<u>Project</u>&#148;
means the building (the &#147;<u>Building</u>&#148;) and the land (the &#147;<u>Land</u>&#148;)
located at 11119 North Torrey Pines Road, San Diego, California.&#160; The &#147;<u>Premises</u>&#148; means that part of the
Project leased to Tenant described in the Schedule&nbsp;and outlined on
Appendix A.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
following schedule&nbsp;(the &#147;<u>Schedule</u>&#148;) is an integral part of this
Lease.&#160; Terms defined in this Schedule&nbsp;shall
have the same meaning throughout the Lease.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:auto;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">SCHEDULE</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:auto;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">1.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Tenant</font></b>:<font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Metabasis Therapeutics, Inc</font></b>., a Delaware
corporation</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">2.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Premises</font></b>:<font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>11119 North Torrey Pines Road</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">3.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Rentable Square Feet of the Premises</font></b>:&#160; Approximately 81,816 rentable square feet,
comprised of 12,078 square feet on the lower level, 37,702 square feet on the
first floor and 32,036 square feet on the second floor, which shall be deemed
conclusively to be the size of the Premises.</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">4.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Tenant&#146;s Proportionate Share of Project</font></b>:&#160; 100%</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">5.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Security Deposit</font></b>:&#160; $152,355.77</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">6.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Tenant&#146;s Real Estate Broker for this Lease</font></b>:&#160; Phase 3 Properties, Inc.</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">7.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Landlord&#146;s Real Estate Broker for this Lease</font></b>:&#160; CB Richard Ellis, Inc.</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">8.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Tenant Improvements, if any</font></b>:&#160; See the Tenant Improvement Agreement attached
hereto as Appendix C.</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">9.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Commencement Date</font></b>:&#160; Upon mutual execution and delivery of this
Lease.</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">10.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Rent Commencement Date</font></b>:&#160; September&nbsp;1, 2005, or the Completion
Date, as defined in Appendix C hereto, if the Completion Date is later.&#160; Landlord and Tenant shall execute a
Commencement Date Confirmation confirming the Commencement Date and the Rent
Commencement Date substantially in the form of Appendix E promptly following
the Commencement Date, and the Rent Commencement Date, as applicable.&#160; On the Rent Commencement Date, Tenant shall
commence paying Base Rent on the portion of the Premises constituting the lower
level and first floor as depicted on Appendix&nbsp;A only (the &#147;<u>Initial
Premises</u>&#148;); as of the 25<sup>th</sup>&nbsp;month of the Term (the &#147;<u>Second
Rent Commencement Date</u>&#148;), Tenant shall commence paying Base Rent on
additional rentable square footage comprising one-half of the second floor of
the Building as depicted on Appendix&nbsp;A (the &#147;<u>Second Expansion Premises</u>&#148;);
as of the 31<sup>st</sup>&nbsp;month of the Term (the &#147;<u>Third Rent
Commencement Date</u>&#148;) Tenant shall commence paying Base Rent on the remaining
portion of the second floor of the Building.</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">11.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:8.5pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Termination Date/Term</font></b>:&#160; 120 months after the Rent Commencement Date,
or if the Rent Commencement Date is not the first day of the month, then 120
months after the first day of the first full month following the Rent Commencement
Date (the</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">

<hr size="2" width="100%" noshade color="gray" align="left">

</font></div>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;<u>Termination
Date</u>&#148;).&#160; The &#147;<u>Term</u>&#148; shall be
the period between the Commencement Date and the Termination Date unless
extended or sooner terminated pursuant to this Lease.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

</font></div>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">*Base
Rent for the first three months following the Rent Commencement Date shall be
subject to an abatement of 50% of Base Rent, notwithstanding anything else
herein to the contrary.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">13.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><b><font style="font-weight:bold;">Sole Permitted Use</font></b>:&#160; Laboratory and general office purposes
consistent with the nature of the Project; however, in no event in violation of
any provision of Section&nbsp;6 of this Lease or of the Rules and Regulations
attached as <u>Appendix&nbsp;B</u> hereto (the &#147;<u>Permitted Use</u>&#148;).</p>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h1 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">1.</font></b><b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><a name="LeaseA"><u>LEASE A</u></a><u>GREEMENT</u></b><font style="color:black;"><font color="black" style="color:windowtext;">.&#160; On the terms stated in this Lease, Landlord
leases the Premises to Tenant, and Tenant leases the Premises from Landlord,
for the Term beginning on the Commencement Date and ending on the Termination
Date unless extended or sooner terminated pursuant to this Lease.&#160; Notwithstanding the occurrence of the
Commencement Date, Tenant&#146;s obligations under this Lease shall not commence
until delivery of the Premises to Tenant.</font></font></h1>

<h1 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></h1>

<h1 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">2.</font></b><b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><a name="Rent"><u>RENT</u></a></b>.</h1>

<h1 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></h1>

<h2 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">A.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Types
of Rent</u><font style="color:black;"><font color="black" style="color:windowtext;">.&#160; Tenant shall pay the following Rent in the
form of a check to Landlord at the following address:</font></font></h2>

<h2 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></h2>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(1)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Base
Rent</u> in monthly installments, without deduction or offset, in advance, the
first monthly installment payable concurrently with the execution of this Lease
and thereafter on or before the first day of each month of the Term in the amount
set forth on the Schedule.</h3>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></h3>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(2)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Operating
Cost Share Rent</u> in an amount equal to the Tenant&#146;s Proportionate Share of
Operating Costs for the applicable Fiscal Year of the Lease, paid monthly in
advance in an estimated amount beginning on the Rent Commencement Date.&#160; Definitions of Operating Costs and Tenant&#146;s
Proportionate Share, and the method for billing and payment of Operating Cost
Share Rent are set forth in Sections 2B, 2C and 2D.</h3>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></h3>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(3)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Tax
Share Rent</u> in an amount equal to the Tenant&#146;s Proportionate Share of Taxes
for the applicable Fiscal Year of this Lease, paid monthly in advance in an
estimated amount beginning on the Rent Commencement Date.&#160; A definition of Taxes and the method for
billing and payment of Tax Share Rent are set forth in Sections 2B, 2C and 2D.</h3>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></h3>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(4)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Additional
Rent</u> in the amount of all costs, expenses, liabilities, and amounts which
Tenant is required to pay under this Lease, excluding Base Rent, Operating Cost
Share Rent, and Tax Share Rent, but including any interest for late payment of
any item of Rent.</h3>

<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(5)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Rent</u>
as used in this Lease means Base Rent, Operating Cost Share Rent, Tax Share
Rent and Additional Rent.&#160; Tenant&#146;s
agreement to pay Rent is an independent covenant, with no right of setoff,
deduction or counterclaim of any kind (except as specifically set forth
herein).</h3>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></h3>

<h2 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">B.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Payment
of Operating Cost Share Rent, Tax Share Rent, and Electricity Share Rent</u>.</h2>

<h2 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></h2>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(1)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Payment
of Estimated Operating Cost Share Rent, Tax Share Rent and Electricity Share
Rent</u>.&#160; Landlord shall estimate the
Operating Costs, Taxes and costs of electricity of the Project by May 15 of
each Fiscal Year, or as soon as reasonably possible thereafter.&#160; Landlord may revise these estimates whenever
it obtains more accurate information, such as the final real estate tax
assessment or tax rate for the Project.</h3>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></h3>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Within
thirty (30) days after receiving the original or revised estimate from Landlord
setting forth an estimate of Operating Costs for a particular Fiscal Year,
Tenant shall pay Landlord one-twelfth (1/12th) of Tenant&#146;s Proportionate Share
of the estimated Operating Costs, multiplied by the number of months that have
elapsed in the applicable Fiscal Year to the date of such payment including the
current month, minus payments previously made by Tenant for the months
elapsed.&#160; On the first day of each month
thereafter, Tenant shall pay Landlord one-twelfth (1/12th) of Tenant&#146;s
Proportionate Share of this estimate, until a new estimate becomes applicable.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Within
thirty (30) days after receiving the original or revised estimate from Landlord
setting forth an estimate of Taxes for a particular Fiscal Year, Tenant shall
pay Landlord one-twelfth (1/12th) of Tenant&#146;s Proportionate Share of the
estimated Tax Share Rent, multiplied by the number of months that have elapsed
in the applicable Fiscal Year to the date of such payment including the current
month, minus payments previously made by Tenant for the months elapsed.&#160; On the first day of each month thereafter,
Tenant shall pay Landlord one-twelfth (1/12th) of Tenant&#146;s Proportionate Share
of this estimate, until a new estimate becomes applicable.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(2)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Correction
of Operating Cost Share Rent</u>.&#160;
Landlord shall deliver to Tenant a report for the previous Fiscal Year
(the &#147;<u>Operating Cost Report</u>&#148;) by May 15 of each year, or as soon as
reasonably possible thereafter, setting forth (a) the actual Operating Costs
incurred, (b)&nbsp; the amount of Operating Cost Share Rent due from Tenant,
and (c)&nbsp;the amount of Operating Cost Share Rent paid by Tenant.&#160; Within thirty (30) days after such delivery,
Tenant shall pay to Landlord the amount due minus the amount paid.&#160; If the amount paid exceeds the amount due, Landlord
shall apply the excess to Tenant&#146;s payments of Rent next coming due, or if no
further payments of Rent are coming due under this Lease because the Lease is
terminating, such excess shall be refunded to Tenant within fifteen (15) days.</h3>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></h3>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(3)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Correction
of Tax Share Rent</u>.&#160; Landlord shall
deliver to Tenant a report for the previous Fiscal Year (the &#147;<u>Tax Report</u>&#148;)
by May 15 of each year, or as soon as reasonably possible thereafter, setting
forth (a) the actual Taxes, (b) the amount of Tax Share Rent due from Tenant,
and (c) the amount of Tax Share Rent paid by Tenant.&#160; Within thirty (30) days after such delivery,
Tenant shall pay to Landlord the amount due from Tenant minus the amount paid
by Tenant.&#160; If the amount paid exceeds
the amount due, Landlord shall apply any excess as a credit</h3>

<h3 align="center" style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></h3>

<h3 align="center" style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">5</font></h3>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">

<hr size="2" width="100%" noshade color="gray" align="left">

</font></h3>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<h3 align="center" style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></h3>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">against Tenant&#146;s payments
of Rent next coming due, or if no further payments of Rent are due under this
Lease because this Lease is terminating, such excess shall be refunded to
Tenant within fifteen (15) days.</font></h3>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></h3>

<h2 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">C.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Definitions</u>.</h2>

<h2 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></h2>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(1)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Included
Operating Costs</u>.&#160; &#147;<u>Operating Costs</u>&#148;
means any expenses, costs and disbursements of any kind other than Taxes, paid
or incurred by Landlord in connection with the management, maintenance,
operation, insurance, repair and other related activities in connection with
any part of the Project and of the personal property, fixtures, machinery,
equipment, systems and apparatus used in connection therewith, including a
property management fee to <font style="color:black;"><font color="black" style="color:windowtext;">Landlord</font></font> of 2.5% of the Base Rent
payable under this Lease.&#160; Operating
Costs shall also include the costs of any capital improvements (each, a &#147;Capital
Item&#148;); provided, that the costs of any Capital Item shall be amortized on a
straight line basis by Landlord, together with interest at 8% per annum, over
the useful life of such item (as determined in accordance with GAAP), and such
amortized costs are only included in Operating Costs for that portion of the
useful life of the Capital Item which falls within the Term.</h3>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></h3>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(2)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Excluded
Operating Costs</u>.&#160; Operating Costs
shall not include:</h3>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></h3>

<h4 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(a)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>interest
and principal payments on mortgages or any other costs related to financing the
Project, or rental payments on any ground lease of the Project;</h4>

<h4 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></h4>

<h4 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(b)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>real
estate brokers&#146; leasing commissions;</h4>

<h4 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></h4>

<h4 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(c)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>legal
fees, space planner fees and advertising expenses incurred with regard to
leasing the Building or portions thereof;</h4>

<h4 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></h4>

<h4 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(d)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>any
cost or expenditure for which Landlord is reimbursed, by insurance proceeds or
otherwise, except by Operating Cost Share Rent;</h4>

<h4 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></h4>

<h4 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(e)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>depreciation
(except on any Included Capital Items);</h4>

<h4 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></h4>

<h4 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(f)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>franchise
or income taxes imposed upon Landlord;</h4>

<h4 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></h4>

<h4 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(g)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>costs
of correcting defects in construction of the Building or Premises or to bring
the Building or Premises into compliance with laws in effect on the Rent
Commencement Date (as opposed to the cost of normal repair, maintenance and
replacement expected with the construction materials and equipment installed in
the Building in light of their specifications);</h4>

<h4 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></h4>

<h4 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(h)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>legal
and auditing fees which are for the benefit of Landlord such as collecting
delinquent rents, preparing tax returns and other financial statements, and
audits other than those incurred in connection with the preparation of reports
required pursuant to Section&nbsp;2B above;</h4>

<h4 align="center" style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></h4>

<h4 align="center" style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">6</font></h4>

<h4 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">

<hr size="2" width="100%" noshade color="gray" align="left">

</font></h4>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<h4 align="center" style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></h4>

<h4 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(i)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>the
wages of any employee for services not related directly to the management,
maintenance, operation and repair of the Building;</h4>

<h4 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></h4>

<h4 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(j)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>fines,
penalties and interest; and</h4>

<h4 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></h4>

<h4 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(k)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>the
costs incurred by <font style="color:black;"><font color="black" style="color:windowtext;">Landlord</font></font> for maintenance, repair
and replacement of the structural components of the roof, the foundation and
exterior, load bearing walls of the Building.</h4>

<h4 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt 1.5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></h4>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(3)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Tenant&#146;s
Proportionate Share</u>.&#160; &#147;<u>Tenant&#146;s
Proportionate Share</u>&#148; means with respect to Operating Costs, Taxes and other
items related to the Project, that percentage set forth in the Schedule&nbsp;as
Tenant&#146;s Proportionate Share of the Project.</h3>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></h3>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(4)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Taxes</u>.&#160; &#147;<u>Taxes</u>&#148; means any and all taxes,
assessments and charges of any kind, general or special, ordinary or
extraordinary, levied against the Project, which Landlord shall pay or become
obligated to pay in connection with the ownership, leasing, renting,
management, use, occupancy, control or operation of the Project or of the
personal property, fixtures, machinery, equipment, systems and apparatus used
in connection therewith.&#160; <font style="color:black;"><font color="black" style="color:windowtext;">Taxes shall
include real estate taxes, personal property taxes, sewer rents, water rents,
special or general assessments, transit taxes, ad valorem taxes, and any tax
levied on the rents hereunder or the interest of Landlord under this Lease (the
&#147;<u>Rent Tax</u>&#148;).&#160; Taxes shall also
include all fees and other costs and expenses paid by Landlord in reviewing any
tax and in seeking a refund or reduction of any Taxes, whether or not the
Landlord is ultimately successful.</font></font></h3>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></h3>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">For
any year, the amount to be included in Taxes shall only be the Taxes imposed
for such year, regardless of when such Taxes are actually paid.&#160; Any refund or other adjustment to any Taxes
by the taxing authority, shall apply during the year in which the adjustment is
made.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Taxes
shall not include any net income, capital, stock, succession, transfer,
franchise, gift, estate, inheritance, unincorporated business association, or
general corporation tax, except to the extent that such tax shall be imposed in
lieu of any portion of Taxes.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Tenant
shall have the right, after 15 days&#146; prior written notice to Landlord, to
contest the amount or validity of any Taxes payable with respect to the
Premises, in whole or in part, by appropriate administrative and legal
proceedings, either in its own name, Landlord&#146;s name or jointly with Landlord,
without any cost or expense to Landlord.&#160;
Tenant may postpone payment of any such contested Taxes pending the
prosecution of such proceedings and any appeals so long as such proceedings
shall operate to prevent the collection of such Taxes (and any fines or
penalties) and the sale of the Premises to satisfy any lien arising out of the
nonpayment of the same.&#160; Tenant, upon the
request of Landlord, shall furnish a bond to Landlord sufficient to secure the
payment of all contested Taxes, costs and expenses in connection therewith as a
pre-condition to undertaking any such contest.&#160;
In lieu of such bond, Tenant may elect to pay such Taxes under protest.&#160; Landlord, at no cost to Landlord, will
reasonably cooperate with Tenant in providing relevant documentation or
information pertaining to such contest, such as appraisals or tax records.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-indent:0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-indent:0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">7</font></p>

<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-indent:0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(5)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Lease
Year</u>.&#160; &#147;<u>Lease Year</u>&#148; means each
consecutive twelve-month period beginning with the Rent Commencement Date (with
the period between the Commencement Date and the Rent Commencement Date deemed
to be part of the first Lease Year).</h3>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></h3>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(6)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Fiscal
Year</u>.&#160; &#147;<u>Fiscal Year</u>&#148; or &#147;<u>fiscal
year</u>&#148; means the calendar year, except that the first fiscal year and the
last fiscal year of the Term may be a partial calendar year.</h3>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></h3>

<h2 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">D.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Computation
of Base Rent and Rent Adjustments</u>.</h2>

<h2 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></h2>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(1)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Prorations</u>.&#160; If this Lease begins on a day other than the
first day of a month, the Base Rent, Operating Cost Share Rent, and Tax Share
Rent shall be prorated for such partial month based on the actual number of
days in such month.&#160; If this Lease begins
on a day other than the first day, or ends on a day other than the last day, of
the Fiscal Year, Operating Cost Share Rent and Tax Share Rent shall be prorated
for the applicable Fiscal Year.</h3>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></h3>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(2)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Default
Interest</u>.&#160; Any sum due from Tenant to
Landlord not paid within five&nbsp;(5) days after notice shall bear interest
from the date due until paid at the lesser of ten percent (10%) per annum or
the maximum rate permitted by law.</h3>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></h3>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(3)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Rent
Adjustments</u>.&#160; The square footage of
the Premises and the Building currently set forth in the Schedule&nbsp;shall be
conclusively deemed to be the actual square footage thereof, subject to
remeasurement as set forth on the Schedule.&#160;
If any Operating Cost paid in one fiscal year relates to more than one
fiscal year, Landlord may proportionately allocate such Operating Cost among
the related fiscal years.</h3>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></h3>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(4)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Books
and Records</u>.&#160; Landlord shall maintain
books and records reflecting the Operating Costs and Taxes in accordance with
sound accounting and management practices.&#160;
Unless Tenant sends to Landlord any written exception to either such
report within said ninety (90) day period, such report shall be deemed final
and accepted by Tenant.&#160; If Tenant makes
a timely exception, Landlord shall cause an independent certified public
accountant with no pre-existing relationship with either Landlord or Tenant,
with at least ten (10) years of experience in auditing the books and records of
commercial office projects, and working on other than a contingent fee
arrangement, and reasonably approved by Tenant to perform an audit of Landlord&#146;s
books and records, the results of which shall be binding on Landlord and Tenant.&#160; Tenant shall pay the reasonable cost of such
audit unless Landlord&#146;s original determination of annual Operating Costs or
Taxes overstated the amounts thereof by more than five percent (5%).&#160; If Landlord&#146;s original determination of
annual Operating Costs or Taxes is overstated by more than five percent (5%),
then Landlord shall pay the cost of such certification.</h3>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></h3>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(5)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Miscellaneous</u>.&#160; So long as Tenant is in default of any
obligation under this Lease beyond any notice and cure period provided herein,
Tenant shall not be entitled to any refund of any amount from Landlord.&#160; If this Lease is terminated for any reason
prior to the annual determination of Operating Cost Share Rent or Tax Share
Rent, either party shall pay the full amount due to the other within thirty
(30) days after Landlord&#146;s notice to Tenant of the amount when it is
determined.&#160; Landlord may commingle any
payments made with respect to Operating Cost Share Rent or Tax Share Rent,
without payment of interest.</h3>

<h3 align="center" style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></h3>

<h3 align="center" style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">8</font></h3>

<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<h3 align="center" style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></h3>

<h1 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">3.</font></b><b><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;font-weight:bold;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><a name="PreparationAndConditionOfPremisesP"><u>PREPARATION AND CONDITION OF
PREMISES; POSSESSION AND SURRENDER OF PREMISES</u>.</a></b></h1>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h2 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">A.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Condition
of Premises</u><font style="color:black;"><font color="black" style="color:windowtext;">.&#160; Except to the extent of
the Initial Improvements set forth on Appendix&nbsp;C and the warranties set
forth therein and in this Lease, Landlord is leasing the Premises to Tenant
absolutely &#147;as is&#148;, without any obligation to alter, remodel, improve, repair
or decorate any part of the Premises.&#160;
Except as set forth in Appendix C or elsewhere in this Lease, Landlord
expressly disclaims any warranty or representation, express or implied, with
respect to the Project or any portion thereof, including, without limitation,
any warranty or representation as to fitness, condition, the existence of any
defect, patent or latent, merchantability, quality or durability.</font></font></h2>

<h2 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></h2>

<h2 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">B.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Tenant&#146;s
Possession</u><font style="color:black;"><font color="black" style="color:windowtext;">.&#160; Except as otherwise specifically set forth
herein, Tenant&#146;s taking possession of any portion of the Premises shall be
conclusive evidence that the Premises was in good order, repair and
condition.&#160; If Landlord authorizes Tenant
to take possession of any part of the Premises prior to the Commencement Date
and Tenant takes such possession for purposes of doing business, all terms of
this Lease shall apply to such pre-Term possession, including Tenant&#146;s
obligation to pay Base Rent.</font></font></h2>

<h2 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></h2>

<h2 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font style="color:black;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">C.</font></font><font style="color:black;"><font size="1" color="black" style="color:windowtext;font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font></font><u>Maintenance</u><font style="color:black;"><font color="black" style="color:windowtext;">.&#160; Subject to Landlord&#146;s obligations
specifically set forth in this Lease, throughout the Term, Tenant shall be
primarily responsible for maintaining the Premises in good order, repair and
condition, loss or damage caused by the elements, ordinary wear and tear, fire
and other casualty excepted, and at the termination of this Lease, or Tenant&#146;s
right to possession, Tenant shall return the Premises to Landlord in
broom-clean, safe, neat and sanitary condition, without any damage, normal wear
and tear excepted.&#160; To the extent Tenant
fails to perform any obligation to repair after applicable notice and cure
periods, Landlord may, but need not, restore the Premises to such condition and
Tenant shall pay the cost thereof.&#160;
Tenant acknowledges that Landlord is leasing the Premises on a &#147;triple
net&#148; basis (which is reflected in the amount of Base Rent Tenant is obligated
to pay), so that Tenant is expected to pay the costs of repair and maintenance
at the Building during the Term.&#160; Notwithstanding,
Landlord shall be responsible (at its sole cost and expense) for repairs to the
structural components of the roof, the load bearing walls and slab floor of the
Building.&#160; Landlord will assign to Tenant
as and when necessary any warranties related to any part of the Premises, or if
such warranties are not assignable, will take reasonable action to enforce such
warranties for the benefit of Tenant.&#160;
Subject to Section&nbsp;2B hereof, Landlord shall maintain the all
portions of the Project outside of the Premises (e.g.&nbsp;parking areas, and
landscaping).</font></font></h2>

<h2 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></h2>

<h2 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">D.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><font style="color:black;"><u><font color="black" style="color:windowtext;">Surrender
of Premises</font></u></font><font style="color:black;"><font color="black" style="color:windowtext;">.&#160; Upon the
expiration of the Term or earlier termination of Tenant&#146;s right of possession,
Tenant shall surrender the Premises to Landlord in good condition, free of
Hazardous Substances brought upon, kept, used, stored, handled, treated,
created, developed, produced, generated in, or released or disposed of from the
Premises by any person other than Landlord, its agents, employees or
contractors, and released of </font></font>any license, clearance or
other authorization of any kind affecting the Premises and issued by any
governmental authority having jurisdiction over the use, storage, handling,
generation, release or disposal of Hazardous Substances in or about the
Premises.&#160; The Premises shall be
surrendered <font style="color:black;"><font color="black" style="color:windowtext;">broom
clean, ordinary wear and tear and casualty loss and condemnation excepted, and
Tenant shall not be responsible for any condition of the Premises which arises
ordinarily with the passage of time</font></font></h2>

<h2 align="center" style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font style="color:black;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></font></h2>

<h2 align="center" style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font style="color:black;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></font></h2>

<h2 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font style="color:black;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">unless Tenant contributed to such
condition by its failure to meet its obligations for repair and maintenance

generator&#148; or similar form required by governmental authority with respect to
the use of Hazardous </font></font>Substances<font style="color:black;"><font color="black" style="color:windowtext;"> on the Premises by Tenant during
the Term.&#160; Tenant hereby appoints
Landlord as its agent in fact for the limited purpose of signing any &#147;hazardous

Hazardous Substances; provided that Landlord hereby covenants to exercise its

any such form after written request by Landlord.&#160; Nothing herein shall be construed to make
Tenant liable for any condition of Hazardous Substances on or around the
Premises which arose prior to the date of delivery of the Premises to Tenant
which Tenant did not cause, contribute to or exacerbate.&#160; At least 6 months prior to the Termination
Date, Tenant shall identify and notify Landlord of all action required to be

termination of the Term, free from any effect from Tenant&#146;s use of Hazardous </font></font>Substances<font style="color:black;"><font color="black" style="color:windowtext;"> in the

and perform such additional procedures as may be deemed reasonably necessary to

effects of Tenant&#146;s use of Hazardous </font></font>Substances<font style="color:black;"><font color="black" style="color:windowtext;"> in the
Premises during the Term.&#160; Landlord shall

preparing the Premises for surrender.&#160;
Tenant shall reimburse Landlord, as Additional Rent, for the actual

consultant to visit the Premises and verify satisfactory completion of the same
but only if Landlord&#146;s environmental consultant determines that Tenant has not
met its obligations hereunder.&#160; </font></font>If

Project are surrendered free from any residual impact from Tenant&#146;s use of
Hazardous Substances, the cost of which actions shall be reimbursed by Tenant
as Additional Rent.&#160; Upon expiration of
this Lease, Tenant shall immediately return to Landlord all keys and/or access
cards to parking, the Project, restrooms or all or any portion of the
Premises.&#160; Any of Tenant&#146;s personal
property which is not removed as required herein shall be deemed abandoned and
may be disposed of by Landlord at Tenant&#146;s expense, and Tenant waives all
claims against Landlord for any damages resulting from Landlord&#146;s disposal of
such personal property.&#160; The obligations
of Tenant under this Section&nbsp;3.D shall survive the expiration or earlier
termination of the Lease.</h2>

without in each instance submitting plans and specifications for the Work to

outside the Premises.&#160; Landlord will be

(a)&nbsp;compromises the base structural components or systems of the Building,
(b) impacts any other tenant&#146;s premises, or (c) is visible from outside the

<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-indent:0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">equipment and personal property and for items which
Landlord requires Tenant to remove at Tenant&#146;s cost at the termination of the
Lease pursuant to Section&nbsp;5E.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The
following requirements shall apply to all Work:</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(1)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Prior

and, at Landlord&#146;s request, security for payment of all costs.</h3>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></h3>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(2)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Tenant
shall perform all Work so as to maintain peace and harmony among other
contractors serving the Project and shall avoid interference with other work to

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></h3>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(3)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>The
Work shall be performed in a good and workmanlike manner, meeting the standard
for construction and quality of materials in the Building, and shall comply
with all insurance requirements and all applicable governmental laws,
ordinances and regulations (&#147;<u>Governmental Requirements</u>&#148;).</h3>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></h3>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(4)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Tenant
shall perform all Work so as to minimize or prevent disruption to other
tenants, and Tenant shall comply with all reasonable requests of Landlord in
response to complaints from other tenants.</h3>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></h3>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(5)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Tenant
shall perform all Work in compliance with Landlord&#146;s reasonable requirements.</h3>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></h3>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(6)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Tenant
shall permit Landlord to monitor all Work.</h3>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></h3>

<h3 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(7)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Upon
completion, Tenant shall furnish Landlord with contractor&#146;s affidavits and full
and final statutory waivers of liens, as-built plans and specifications, and
receipted bills covering all labor and materials, and all other close-out
documentation required in Landlord&#146;s policies, rules and procedures for
construction projects.</h3>

<h3 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:1.0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></h3>

<h2 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">B.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>Damage
to Systems</u><font style="color:black;"><font color="black" style="color:windowtext;">.&#160; If any part of the mechanical, electrical or
other systems in the Premises shall be damaged, Tenant shall promptly notify
Landlord, and Tenant shall repair such damage.&#160;
Landlord may also at any reasonable time, after reasonable prior notice,
make any repairs or alterations which Landlord deems necessary for the safety
or protection of the Project, or which Landlord is required to make by any
court or pursuant to any Governmental Requirement.&#160; Tenant shall at its expense make all other
repairs necessary to keep the Premises, and Tenant&#146;s fixtures and personal
property, in good order, condition and repair; to the extent Tenant fails to do
so, Landlord may make such repairs itself.&#160;
The actual reasonable cost of any repairs made by Landlord on account of
Tenant&#146;s default, or on account of the mis-use or neglect by Tenant or its
invitees, contractors or agents anywhere in the Project, shall become
Additional Rent payable by Tenant on demand.</font></font></h2>

<h2 style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></h2>

<h2 style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">C.</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font><u>No
Liens</u><font style="color:black;"><font color="black" style="color:windowtext;">.&#160; Tenant has no authority to cause or permit
any lien or encumbrance of any kind to affect Landlord&#146;s interest in the
Project; any such lien or encumbrance shall attach to</font></font></h2>

<h2 align="center" style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font style="color:black;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></font></h2>

<h2 align="center" style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font style="color:black;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">12</font></font></h2>
